pse_effect_access_ui_from_short_window = {
    potential = {
        is_scope_type = country
        has_country_flag = pse_top_bar_enabled
    }
    allow = {

    }
    effect = {
        custom_tooltip = pse_power_text_title
        custom_tooltip = pse_power_text_icon_desc
    }
}

pse_effect_access_ui_from_short = {
    potential = {
        is_scope_type = country
        has_country_flag = pse_top_bar_enabled
    }
    allow = {

    }
    effect = {
        custom_tooltip = edict_pse_psi_ruler_ui_tooltip
        hidden_effect = {
            country_event = {
                id = pse.1000
            }
        }
    }
}

pse_effect_top_bar_switch = {
    potential = {
        always = yes
    }
    allow = {

    }
    effect = {
        custom_tooltip = pse_top_bar_switch_tooltip
        hidden_effect = {
            if = {
                limit = {
                    NOT = {
                        has_country_flag = pse_top_bar_enabled
                    }
                }
                set_country_flag = pse_top_bar_enabled
            }
            else = {
                remove_country_flag = pse_top_bar_enabled
            }
        }
    }
}

        }
    }
}

    potential = {
        NOT = {
            has_country_flag = pse_notify_enabled

        is_scope_type = country
    }
    allow = {

    }
    effect = {
        custom_tooltip = pse_notify_enable_tooltip
        hidden_effect = {
            set_country_flag = pse_notify_enabled
        }
    }
}

pse_desc_effect_text = {
    potential = {
        always = yes
    }
    allow = {

    }
    effect = {
        change_variable = {
            which = pse_power
            value = 50
        }
        country_event = { #Calc require power cost
            id = pse.2004
        }
    }
}

pse_close_window_effect = { #CLEAR ALL variable for avoiding calc bug
    potential = {
        always = yes
    }
    allow = {

    }
    effect = {
        hidden_effect = {
            country_event = { #Reset zro calc
                id = pse.1999
            }
            country_event = { #Deselect main
                id = pse.2002
            }  
            country_event = { #Deselect power
                id = pse.2003
            }
            country_event = { #Calc require power cost reset
                id = pse.2005
            }
        }
    }
}

###LEADER POWER###
    pse_power_botton_leader_find_button_effect = { #cost 50
        potential = {
            has_country_flag = pse_power_leader_main_selected
        }
        allow = {
            custom_tooltip = pse_power_botton_leader_find_title
            custom_tooltip = pse_power_botton_leader_find_desc
            custom_tooltip = {
                fail_text = pse_power_botton_selected_tooltip
                NOT = {
                    has_country_flag = pse_power_leader_find_selected
                }
            }
            custom_tooltip = { #More intuitive visual
                fail_text = pse_power_botton_not_enough_power_and_zro_to_cast
                check_variable = {
                    which = pse_power
                    value >= 35 
                }
            }
            custom_tooltip = {
                fail_text = pse_power_botton_leader_find_cant_fine_one
                any_owned_leader = {
                    species = {
                        OR = {
                            has_trait = trait_latent_psionic
                            has_trait = trait_psionic
                        }
                    }
                    NOT = {
                        OR = {
                            has_trait = leader_trait_admiral_psionic
                            has_trait = leader_trait_general_psionic
                            has_trait = leader_trait_governor_psionic
                            has_trait = leader_trait_scientist_psionic
                            has_trait = leader_trait_ruler_psionic
                            has_trait = leader_trait_admiral_chosen
                            has_trait = leader_trait_general_chosen
                            has_trait = leader_trait_governor_chosen
                            has_trait = leader_trait_scientist_chosen
                            has_trait = leader_trait_ruler_chosen
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
            hidden_trigger = {
                NOT = {
                    has_country_flag = pse_power_leader_find_cooldown
                }
            }
            if = {
                limit = {
                    has_country_flag = pse_power_leader_find_cooldown
                }
                if = {
                    limit = {
                        has_country_flag = pse_power_leader_find_cooldown_360
                    }
                    custom_tooltip = pse_power_cooldown_360_5year_desc
                }
                else_if = {
                    limit = {
                        has_country_flag = pse_power_leader_find_cooldown_720
                    }
                    custom_tooltip = pse_power_cooldown_720_5year_desc
                }
                else_if = {
                    limit = {
                        has_country_flag = pse_power_leader_find_cooldown_1080
                    }
                    custom_tooltip = pse_power_cooldown_1080_5year_desc
                }
                else_if = {
                    limit = {
                        has_country_flag = pse_power_leader_find_cooldown_1440
                    }
                    custom_tooltip = pse_power_cooldown_1440_5year_desc
                }
                else_if = {
                    limit = {
                        has_country_flag = pse_power_leader_find_cooldown_1470
                    }
                    custom_tooltip = pse_power_cooldown_1470_5year_desc
                }
                else_if = {
                    limit = {
                        has_country_flag = pse_power_leader_find_cooldown_1500
                    }
                    custom_tooltip = pse_power_cooldown_1500_5year_desc
                }
                else_if = {
                    limit = {
                        has_country_flag = pse_power_leader_find_cooldown_1530
                    }
                    custom_tooltip = pse_power_cooldown_1530_5year_desc
                }
                else_if = {
                    limit = {
                        has_country_flag = pse_power_leader_find_cooldown_1560
                    }
                    custom_tooltip = pse_power_cooldown_1560_5year_desc
                }
                else_if = {
                    limit = {
                        has_country_flag = pse_power_leader_find_cooldown_1590
                    }
                    custom_tooltip = pse_power_cooldown_1590_5year_desc
                }
                else_if = {
                    limit = {
                        has_country_flag = pse_power_leader_find_cooldown_1620
                    }
                    custom_tooltip = pse_power_cooldown_1620_5year_desc
                }
                else_if = {
                    limit = {
                        has_country_flag = pse_power_leader_find_cooldown_1650
                    }
                    custom_tooltip = pse_power_cooldown_1650_5year_desc
                }
                else_if = {
                    limit = {
                        has_country_flag = pse_power_leader_find_cooldown_1680
                    }
                    custom_tooltip = pse_power_cooldown_1680_5year_desc
                }
                else_if = {
                    limit = {
                        has_country_flag = pse_power_leader_find_cooldown_1710
                    }
                    custom_tooltip = pse_power_cooldown_1710_5year_desc
                }
                else_if = {
                    limit = {
                        has_country_flag = pse_power_leader_find_cooldown_1740
                    }
                    custom_tooltip = pse_power_cooldown_1740_5year_desc
                }
                else_if = {
                    limit = {
                        has_country_flag = pse_power_leader_find_cooldown_1770
                    }
                    custom_tooltip = pse_power_cooldown_1770_5year_desc
                }
                else_if = {
                    limit = {
                        has_country_flag = pse_power_leader_find_cooldown_1800
                    }
                    custom_tooltip = pse_power_cooldown_1800_5year_desc
                }
            }
        }
        effect = {
            custom_tooltip = pse_power_botton_leader_find_title
            custom_tooltip = pse_power_botton_leader_find_desc
            custom_tooltip = pse_botton_select_text
            hidden_effect = {
                country_event = { #Deselect power
                    id = pse.2003
                }
                country_event = { #Reset zro calc
                    id = pse.1999
                }
                set_country_flag = pse_power_selected_one_of_them
                set_country_flag = pse_power_leader_find_selected
                set_variable = {
                    which = pse_power_cost
                    value = 50
                }
                country_event = { #Calc require power cost
                    id = pse.2004
                }
            }
        }
    }
    pse_power_botton_leader_find_button_effect_tooltip = {
        potential = {
            has_country_flag = pse_power_leader_find_selected
        }
        allow = {
        }
        effect = {
        }
    }
    pse_power_botton_leader_find_button_effect_cooldown = {
        potential = {
            has_country_flag = pse_power_leader_main_selected
            has_country_flag = pse_power_leader_find_cooldown
        }
        allow = {
        }
        effect = {

    pse_power_botton_break_unity_button_effect = { #cost 115
        potential = {
            has_country_flag = pse_power_break_main_selected
        }
        allow = {

                fail_text = pse_power_botton_selected_tooltip

                }
            }
            custom_tooltip = { #More intuitive visual

                    which = pse_power
                    value >= 70
                }
            }
            custom_tooltip = {
                fail_text = pse_power_botton_break_dont_have_vaild_neighbor
                any_neighbor_country = {
                    has_communications = root

                        is_berserker_to = root
                        is_belligerent_to = root
                        is_angry_to = root
                        is_domineering_to = root
                        is_unfriendly_to = root
                        is_hostile_to = root
                        is_rival = root
                        is_harming_relations_with = root
                        is_at_war_with = root

                        is_same_empire = root

    pse_power_botton_chosen_worship_button_effect = { #cost 215
        potential = {
            has_country_flag = pse_power_chosen_main_selected
        }
        allow = {
            custom_tooltip = pse_power_botton_chosen_worship_title
            custom_tooltip = pse_power_botton_chosen_worship_desc
            custom_tooltip = {
                fail_text = pse_power_botton_selected_tooltip
                NOT = {
                    has_country_flag = pse_power_chosen_worship_selected
                }
            }
            custom_tooltip = { #More intuitive visual
                fail_text = pse_power_botton_not_enough_power_and_zro_to_cast
                check_variable = {
                    which = pse_power
                    value >= 150
                }
            }
            custom_tooltip = {
                fail_text = pse_power_botton_gestalt_consciousness_cannot
                NOT = {
                    has_ethic = ethic_gestalt_consciousness
                }  
            }
            custom_tooltip = {
                fail_text = pse_power_botton_chosen_shroud_upset
                NOT = {
                    has_country_flag = pse_power_chosen_shroud_nevermind
                }
            }
            custom_tooltip = {
                fail_text = pse_power_botton_break_dont_have_vaild_neighbor
                any_neighbor_country = {
                    has_communications = root
                    OR = {

pse_use_zro_discount_calc_plus = {
    potential = {
        always = yes
    }
    allow = {
        custom_tooltip = pse_zro_discount_plus_tooltip
        custom_tooltip = {
            fail_text = pse_select_power_text_select_one_of_them_first
            has_country_flag = pse_power_selected_one_of_them
        }
        custom_tooltip = {
            fail_text = pse_zro_discount_maxed
            check_variable = {
                which = pse_zro_discount_count
                value < 3
            }
        }
        custom_tooltip = {
            fail_text = pse_power_botton_cleanse_cannot_use_zro
            NOT = {
                has_country_flag = pse_power_cleanse_main_selected
            }
        }
        has_technology = tech_pse_zro_1
    }
    effect = {
        custom_tooltip = pse_zro_discount_plus_tooltip
        hidden_effect = {
            change_variable = {
                which = pse_zro_discount_count
                value = 1
            }
            country_event = { #Zro discount calc
                id = pse.2001
            } 
        }
       
    }
}

###PSE MONTHLY POWER NUM

    pse_monthly_power_num_tooltip = {
        potential = {
            always = yes
        }
        allow = {
            custom_tooltip = {
                fail_text = pse_power_increase_month_desc
                always = no
            } 
            custom_tooltip = {
                fail_text = pse_power_increase_month_modifier_base
                always = no
            } 
            custom_tooltip = {
                success_text = pse_power_increase_month_modifier_hive_mind
                has_authority = auth_hive_mind
            }
            custom_tooltip = {
                success_text = pse_power_increase_month_modifier_ruler1
                leader = {
                    leader_class = ruler
                    NOR = {
                        has_trait = leader_trait_ruler_chosen
                        has_trait = leader_trait_ruler_psionic
                    }
                    species = {
                        has_trait = trait_latent_psionic
                        NOT = {
                            has_trait = trait_psionic
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
            custom_tooltip = {
                success_text = pse_power_increase_month_modifier_ruler2
                leader = {
                    leader_class = ruler
                    has_trait = leader_trait_ruler_psionic
                    NOT = {
                        has_trait = leader_trait_ruler_chosen
                    }
                }
            }
            custom_tooltip = {
                success_text = pse_power_increase_month_modifier_ruler3
                leader = {
                    leader_class = ruler
                    has_trait = leader_trait_ruler_chosen
                }
                NOT = {
                    has_country_flag = pse_power_chosen_shroud_nevermind
                }
            }
            custom_tooltip = {
                success_text = pse_power_increase_month_modifier_ap1
                has_ascension_perk = ap_mind_over_matter
            }
            custom_tooltip = {
                success_text = pse_power_increase_month_modifier_ap2
                has_ascension_perk = ap_transcendence
            }
            
            custom_tooltip = {
                success_text = pse_power_increase_month_modifier_leader1
                check_variable = {
                    which = pse_leader_num
                    value > 9
                }
                check_variable = {
                    which = pse_leader_num
                    value < 20
                }
            }

            custom_tooltip = {
                success_text = pse_power_increase_month_modifier_leader2
                check_variable = {
                    which = pse_leader_num
                    value > 19
                }
                check_variable = {
                    which = pse_leader_num
                    value < 30
                }
            }

            custom_tooltip = {
                success_text = pse_power_increase_month_modifier_leader3
                check_variable = {
                    which = pse_leader_num
                    value > 29
                }
                check_variable = {
                    which = pse_leader_num
                    value < 40
                }
            }

            custom_tooltip = {
                success_text = pse_power_increase_month_modifier_leader4
                check_variable = {
                    which = pse_leader_num
                    value > 39
                }
            }

            custom_tooltip = {
                success_text = pse_power_increase_month_modifier_job1
                num_assigned_jobs = {
                    job = telepath
                    value > 3
                }
                num_assigned_jobs = {
                    job = telepath
                    value < 8
                }
            }
            custom_tooltip = {
                success_text = pse_power_increase_month_modifier_job2
                num_assigned_jobs = {
                    job = telepath
                    value > 7
                }
                num_assigned_jobs = {
                    job = telepath
                    value < 12
                }
            }
            custom_tooltip = {
                success_text = pse_power_increase_month_modifier_job3
                num_assigned_jobs = {
                    job = telepath
                    value > 11
                }
                num_assigned_jobs = {
                    job = telepath
                    value < 16
                }
            }
            custom_tooltip = {
                success_text = pse_power_increase_month_modifier_job4
                num_assigned_jobs = {
                    job = telepath
                    value > 15
                }
            }
            custom_tooltip = {
                success_text = pse_power_increase_month_modifier_tech1
                has_technology = tech_pse_power_1
                NOR = {
                    has_technology = tech_pse_power_2
                    has_technology = tech_pse_power_3
                }
            }
            custom_tooltip = {
                success_text = pse_power_increase_month_modifier_tech2
                has_technology = tech_pse_power_1
                has_technology = tech_pse_power_2
                NOT = {
                    has_technology = tech_pse_power_3
                }
            }
            custom_tooltip = {
                success_text = pse_power_increase_month_modifier_tech3
                has_technology = tech_pse_power_1
                has_technology = tech_pse_power_2
                has_technology = tech_pse_power_3
            }
            custom_tooltip = {
                success_text = pse_power_increase_month_modifier_zro_crystal
                has_relic = r_zro_crystal
            }
            custom_tooltip = {
                success_text = pse_power_increase_month_modifier_psy_siphon1
                has_global_flag = gigastructures_enabled
                OR = {
                    has_megastructure = psychic_hypersiphon_1
                    has_megastructure = psychic_hypersiphon_2
                }
                NOR = {
                    has_megastructure = psychic_hypersiphon_3
                    has_megastructure = psychic_hypersiphon_3_aeternum
                }
            }
            custom_tooltip = {
                success_text = pse_power_increase_month_modifier_psy_siphon2
                has_global_flag = gigastructures_enabled
                OR = {
                    has_megastructure = psychic_hypersiphon_3
                    has_megastructure = psychic_hypersiphon_3_aeternum
                }
            }
            custom_tooltip = {
                success_text = pse_power_increase_month_modifier_edict
                has_edict = pse_psi_power
            }
            custom_tooltip = {
                success_text = pse_power_increase_month_modifier_zero_corruption
                has_technology = tech_pse_circle_1
                check_variable = {
                    which = pse_corruption
                    value < 0.01
                }
            }
        }
        effect = {
            
        }
